mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">前言：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自本月度报告的第<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，本报告全新改版。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">同时，鉴于</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">中国人权捍卫者（<span lang="EN-US">CHRD</span>）</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">所属的</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库</span></b></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">已将本网月度报告中所涉及的良心犯均全部收录，因此，我们从<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，将绝大多数本月没有动态信息的良心犯简历不再在月度报告里显示。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">我们仍将把在押良心犯名录附于报告内，读者可以根据姓名登录进入《中国大陆良心犯数据库》</span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">查询所有相关信息，非常便捷。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日共收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3405</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">8</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年多来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">八年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">以此</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">八年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网邮箱：</span></b></span><a href="mailto:wqw2011@gmail.com"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">wqw2011@gmail.com</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 0; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo24; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">106</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整八年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">4</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千字</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">57</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人已被</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放或取保获释。并获悉有被羁押的<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">16</span>人狱中有新动态，</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留、强迫失踪的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">22</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">33</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1690</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk162449568"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">二</span></b></a></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、本月获悉上期名录中刑满释放的<span lang="EN-US">57</span>人的名单及简历<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1/</span></b></span><a name="_Hlk172959886"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李明华</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">辽宁省葫芦岛市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁。原是葫芦岛市南票区大窝铺村的民办教师，执教有四、五年，自办幼儿园有十年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，她开始修炼法轮功。李明华老太太<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日乘车去看怀孕的女儿，安检时被抓捕、随后遭抄家，后被关押在葫芦岛看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日获悉：李明华于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被葫芦岛连山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，后李明华已被转监辽宁省第二女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底安秀荣被抓捕，一直被关押在顺义区看守所，曾被密集提审并遭到背铐。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">3/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">白雪松：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省鞍山市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日午后，居住在鞍山市铁西区民政局附近的史颜影，在鞍山市一所养老院工作期间被抓捕，并被关押到岫岩看守所。她家中电脑、打印机等私有物品被抄走。警方于次日抓捕了去她家的白雪松。白雪松、史颜影，被警察抓捕、关押构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，史颜影被立山法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、白雪松被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/2/450323.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/2/450323.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span><a name="_Hlk172960500"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">常玮平</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1984</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，陕西省宝鸡市凤翔县城关镇周家门前村人，原陕西立刚律师事务所执业律师，人权律师，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">早年曾就读于重庆大学；毕业后，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，通过一系列的律师资格自修和考试，最终获取律师执业资格证，后在陕西立刚律师事务所成为正式律师；工作期间，不仅曾代理多起公益诉讼（含艾滋歧视、乙肝歧视、性别歧视等）案件，亦曾代理过多起诸如“无锡<span lang="EN-US">4</span>·<span lang="EN-US">13</span>寻衅滋事案”、“无锡访民王金娣寻衅滋事案”、“南京王健寻衅滋事案”等敏感人权及弱势群体维权案件；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因此而被陕西宝鸡司法局停业<span lang="EN-US"> 3 </span>个月；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22 </span>日，其律师资格证被当地律师事务所注销；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，在停业期满后，其基本处于无法在其他律师事务所获得工作机会的状态，因其曾在陕西省境内与至少<span lang="EN-US">10</span>家律师事务所接洽，但皆不顺利，或即将签约时临时变卦，或虽签约后又突然解除合约；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因参加了一个与多名维权律师和异见人士在厦门的非正式私人聚会，后因被中共官方知晓后定性为“厦门聚会案”，多人遭严打狠抓，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其亦被陕西省宝鸡市警方跨省抓走，并被以“危害国家安全”为由指定居所监视居住；后被取保候审，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又因对外发视频称其在拘押期间，遭受酷刑，即每天（<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时<span lang="EN-US">/</span>次）都把他绑在一种叫做“老虎凳”的刑具上，连续审问<span lang="EN-US">16</span>次，致其右手拇指到食指至今都毫无知觉，且在取保获释后仍受到严密监视等，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，随再次被陕西省宝鸡市警方抓走，后被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被宝鸡市检察院以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案在陕西省宝鸡市凤县法院秘密开庭，其妻子前往要求参加旁听，遭警方恶意围堵；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，终被宝鸡市凤县法院一审以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。此前被羁押于宝鸡市凤县看守所。现在已经转监到陕西省渭南监狱。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">程渊：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省长沙市人，广东省深圳市常驻居民，中国民间公益机构“长沙富能”创办人（之一）、工作人员，乙肝病毒携带者、艾滋病病毒感染者等群体维权诉讼代理人，中国在押政治犯。因从事公益维权活动<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余年，曾代理过<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多起乙肝病毒携带者、艾滋病病毒感染者维权诉讼案，颇受弱势群体爱戴欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾首例成功代理江西省进贤县艾滋就业歧视案，为当事人争得赔偿，经多家媒体报导而广为人知，但亦引起中共当局的高度警觉及跟踪监控；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，突然被湖南省长沙市国家安全局警方从深圳跨境带走，并被旋即以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；审讯期间，被多次问及其在长沙富能所做的工作内容、资金来源及其近期外出活动（含去香港，与香港记者录像等）都做些什么等细节详情；据悉，被抓当天，其家属多受牵连，其妻竟被戴黑头套遭无辜审讯长达<span lang="EN-US">17</span>小时，其<span lang="EN-US">3</span>岁半幼女遭惊吓，夜晚睡觉出现抽搐和梦呓，白天表现惊恐异常，其兄程浩、其老父亲等均遭警告恐吓；其代理律师欲了解案件详情遭绝，仅告知其罪名及法定的拘留期限；<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转正式逮捕。后遭起诉，并被遭强行委派官派律师，对家属严密封锁，拒不见面。家属外界都无法获知案情进展。已经开庭审理，家属仍然对信息一无所知。被羁押于湖南省国家安全厅看守所。长沙富能发起人程渊的妻子施明磊综合各渠道信息，获悉长沙公益仨程渊、吴葛健雄、刘大志三人已在北京时间<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午被长沙市中级法院判决，吴葛健雄被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刘大志被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉：长沙富能公益案之程渊被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑，</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">现在于湖南赤山监狱服刑。程渊在赤山监狱被关禁闭三个月，强迫劳动暴瘦<span lang="EN-US">12</span>斤头发全白<span lang="EN-US">, </span>程渊家人收到家书伤心落泪<b>。</b>刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">&nbsp; &nbsp;</span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_98.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">重庆市永川区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月生。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省佳木斯市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生。家住佳木斯市向阳区红旗路北段林机小区红旗佳苑，户籍所在地是佳木斯市郊区。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">11/</span></b></span><a name="_Hlk172961813"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，四川西昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，黄彪买东西回来，被国安蹲坑抓捕控制后抄家，警察抄走大量私人物品和几万人民币。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日黄彪被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索处罚金<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黄敏：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">10</span>日被视频开庭，八个月后<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">14/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，辽宁锦州法轮功学员。高中文化，辽宁省锦州市人，曾经在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被判刑过三年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时许，黄素芹在辽宁省锦州市古塔区早市附近散发真相资料，被抓捕，又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，可能已经被劫持到辽宁女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/12/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-439959.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">15/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">简兰英：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">45</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">岁，家住乐山市中区水口镇谢村。她于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年因病开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，帅惠兰、简兰英去夹江县农村民宅发送法轮功真相资料，被夹江县国保大队警察抓捕、抄家，被送到乐山看守所关押。帅惠兰、简兰英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现被关押于成都龙泉女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E5%B8%85%E6%83%A0%E5%85%B0%E3%80%81%E7%AE%80%E5%85%B0%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E6%9D%B3%E6%97%A0%E9%9F%B3%E4%BF%A1-445293.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E5%B8%85%E6%83%A0%E5%85%B0%E3%80%81%E7%AE%80%E5%85%B0%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E6%9D%B3%E6%97%A0%E9%9F%B3%E4%BF%A1-445293.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">16/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李翠婷：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年出生，香港油尖旺区人，文员，香港逃犯条例修订草案（俗称“送中条例”、“逃犯条例”或“引渡条例”）反对者，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>·<span lang="EN-US">1</span>尖沙咀抗议者，香港理工大学抗议学生的声援者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因中共当局在香港推出“逃犯条例修订草案”，遭到香港民众普遍反对，遂掀起“反送中”运动，并由香港民间人权阵线发起「没有国庆，只有国殇」游行，以期在庆祝中华人民共和国成立<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年大会期间同步进行示威，由港岛铜锣湾游行至中环，向港府表达反对“逃犯条例修订草案”的要求，但却遭到香港警方的明确反对，并被公众集会及游行上诉委员会上诉后被驳回；不料港府官方的这一反对立场立即激怒了要求高度自治，“真普选”、“真自由”的香港民众的强烈反对，故有大批民众决定自我承担法律后果，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-11</span>月（国庆节期间及之后数十日），在港多区自行发起“反对逃犯条例修订草案”示威抗议行动；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李翠婷与约<span lang="EN-US">100</span>名示威者在声援被实弹警察围城的香港理工大学（以下简称“理大”）抗议学生时，在突破警方封锁线从校内逃走时，被女警打倒在地，并被以“参与暴力”为由野蛮拘捕；之后又被警方指控，因参与声援抗议行动时向警方“投掷汽油弹”，并与多人统一“身穿深色衣物、戴面罩及手持雨伞等”，故被以涉嫌“参与暴动罪”交由香港区域法院提堂聆讯；此间虽有暂时交保释放，但后又被收监，并与同期被捕的另<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名抗议<span lang="EN-US">/</span>声援者（共<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人案）一同转交到香港西九龙裁判法院受审；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其终被该法院以“暴动罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日；另<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人亦被以“暴动罪”和“管有攻击性武器罪”分别判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月至<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年不等刑期。目前在香港罗湖惩教所（香港新界上水河上乡路<span lang="EN-US">163</span>号）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/49.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/9/%E6%B9%96%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%91%E6%A2%A6%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9D%8E%E5%B9%BF%E6%B8%85%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441090.html"><span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，岳峰派出所再次抓捕了李维萍。姐姐李亚萍当时外出，得知消息后被迫流离失所。李维萍现被关押在闽清县拘留所，拘留十四天后，又被转到福州市第二看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被批捕。李维萍被关押近两年后，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日遭马尾区法院庭审。后得知，马尾区法院对她判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：福州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生，系福建省农科院耕作所退休女职工。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘强<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，刘强等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括刘强在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。刘强被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" lang="EN-US">27</span>日被恒山区小恒山派出所警察闯入在鸡东县的家中抄家、抓捕、构陷。后得知，他被鸡东县法院判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省仙桃市法轮功学员，女。刘艳秋因坚持修炼法轮大法，多次遭中共人员骚扰、抓捕。刘艳秋和丈夫欧阳章国曾于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被绑架到武汉汤逊湖洗脑班迫害，欧阳章国因遭迫害严重，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年离世，年仅<span lang="EN-US">38</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日晚，湖北省仙桃市法轮功学员杨冬梅、刘艳秋在胡场镇发放法轮功资料时，被胡场镇派出所警察抓捕、劫持到仙桃市拘留所。杨冬梅被拘留十五天，但<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被转刑拘。刘艳秋后被拘留十天，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日回家；刘艳秋于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日再次被胡场派出所警察欺骗、抓捕，并被刑事拘留。两位法轮功学员被关押到仙桃市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日两人遭仙桃市法院庭审，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被判刑：杨冬梅被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>元，刘艳秋被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；两人已向湖北省汉江中级法院上诉。刘艳秋刑期至<span lang="EN-US">:2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/01/12.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西省九江市法轮功学员，都昌县人。柳秋生原来在都昌县调查队从事统计调查工作（公务员）。因为坚持信仰真善忍，遭迫害被开除公职，没有生活来源。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，柳秋生遭抓捕。非法抄家时抄收现金六万元还有存款和五万美元存单。构陷编造的罪名是“里通外国”，其实是柳秋生家中房屋拆迁款，柳秋生在银行的同学帮助存了美元存单，取不了，美元只是利息高点，这笔钱是留给儿子读大学用的。当局给柳秋生强按的罪名是“里通外国”，<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被九江市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">28/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">龙克海：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1966</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，又名龙刻海，甘肃省徽县嘉陵镇嘉陵村人，基督徒，陕西省宝鸡市长驻居民，民主维权公民，中国曾押政治犯。因为人急公好义，忧国忧民，且信仰基督教，经常参加成都秋雨之福教会的聚会活动，随广受他人赞誉；积极参与各种公民圈活动而曾数次遭到警方“喝茶”、警告；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因民主聚会而被甘肃省徽县警方以“寻衅滋事罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；获释后，因不断向当地法院提出抗诉并要求警方予以国家赔偿，遭到当局的进一步憎恨和报复；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被陕西省宝鸡市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕，后转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案件被地方检察院起诉至陕西省宝鸡市渭滨区法院，指控其在<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>发布和转发一系列诽谤侮辱中共领导人及辱骂中国共产党的言论信息，严重破坏社会秩序，因而构成寻衅滋事罪；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其案在陕西省宝鸡市渭滨区法院不公开审理；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，在不允许家属旁听的情况下，被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服，提起上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，经陕西省宝鸡市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，刑满释放。此前羁押于宝鸡市渭滨区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，甘肃陇南徽县民主维权人士龙克海被甘肃国保从宝鸡带走后，一直没有讯息。后获悉，龙克海已被刑拘。有朋友打通甘肃国宝电话得知，确定龙已被刑拘。国保不愿透露罪名，只说刑拘通知书已给龙的亲属。朋友估计罪名是寻衅滋事罪，可能与龙克海前阵前往陕西凤县围观常玮平开庭有关。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2022</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日甘徽县法院以犯寻衅滋事罪判龙克海有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年， 刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。目前龙克海被羁押在甘肃徽县看守所<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_71.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">哈尔滨市法轮功学员、女，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生。她从黑龙江省农垦师范学院毕业后，在哈尔滨市第六十四中学任教。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日早晨，吕巍在家里被哈尔滨市南岗区燎原派出所、铁路派出所和保健路派出所三个派出所的十几个警察抓捕了，同时抄家。被关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日遭庭审。后被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年</span>，罚金五千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省巴中市法轮功学员，女，巴中市统计局公务员（主任科员）。彭桦英女士，在街上给人讲法轮功真相时，被不明真相的人恶意举报，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/2/450322.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">32/</span></b></span><a name="_Hlk172962832"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林白城市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日发放法轮功资料，被白城市公安局抓捕，被关押在白城市看守所。看守所不让家属见面，家属担忧戚凤珍的身体情况。在被非法关押、被构陷大半年后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年过年前夕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。戚凤珍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">33/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁，家住乐山市中区杨湾乡唐村。她于一九九六年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，帅惠兰、简兰英去夹江县农村民宅发送法轮功真相资料，被夹江县国保大队警察抓捕、抄家，被送到乐山看守所关押。帅惠兰、简兰英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现被关押于成都龙泉女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E5%B8%85%E6%83%A0%E5%85%B0%E3%80%81%E7%AE%80%E5%85%B0%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E6%9D%B3%E6%97%A0%E9%9F%B3%E4%BF%A1-445293.html"><b><span 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/23/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E5%B8%85%E6%83%A0%E5%85%B0%E3%80%81%E7%AE%80%E5%85%B0%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E6%9D%B3%E6%97%A0%E9%9F%B3%E4%BF%A1-445293.html</span></b></a></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">34/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宋昌平：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省德惠市法轮功学员，家住吉林省德惠市达家沟镇五家子大队四社。宋昌平的丈夫常年在外地打工，大儿子因糖尿病严重，失去劳动能力，小儿子患抑郁症，不能工作，平时家里全由宋昌平照顾，两个年幼的孙女也需要她照顾。为了陪孩子读书，她在德惠市龙珠私立学校做保洁。因她对学生讲法轮功真相，被王姓女校长恶告。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被警察抓捕。后宋昌平被关押到长春第四看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月她被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/23/443976.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/23/443976.html</span></b></a></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">35/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙秀丽：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> 广州法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，黑龙江省肇东市人，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日因制作和发放法轮功资料在广州被抓捕。她被抓捕前在广州市天河区火锅店打工。广州市海珠区法院<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月对孙秀丽判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金一万五千元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/21/459037.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/21/459037.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">36/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙秀英</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：吉林农安县法轮功学员。女、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝、高晓歧、蔡玉英、吴冬梅、于姣茹、单为和、赵秀兰、孙秀英、张敬元、孙凤仙、冯立齐、吕相富、董秀辉等<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">22</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：孙秀英被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">37/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">田淑兰：</span></b></span><a name="_Hlk52322917"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">唐山市开平区越河乡西塔村法轮功学员田世胜、田淑兰夫妇，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日早晨被警察闯入家中抓捕，两人被秘密开庭，田世胜被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、田淑兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。</span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">田世胜于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被关押到河北省监狱管理局冀东分局第四监狱。田淑兰于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被绑架至河北省女子监狱。田淑兰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">38/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">童雪升：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广州法轮功学员。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1984</span>年生，福建省三明市清流县人。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，十三岁的童雪升在集美轻工业学校读书时开始修炼法轮功。二十多年来，童雪升因坚持修炼法轮功，屡遭中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，十六岁的童雪升被迫从天津轻工学院退学，并被拘留四十天。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，十七岁的童雪升在儒江劳教所被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，二十一岁时，童雪升被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在闽西监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，童雪升被广州市天河区公安分局和棠下派出所警察抓捕，关押到广州市天河看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被广州市海珠区法院判刑，童雪升获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/21/450994.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/21/450994.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">39/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王健：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市法轮功学员，女，一九八九年出生，兰州交通大学本科生，她毕业后任哈尔滨铁路集团公司宾县分公司助理工程师。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，王健从宾县家中去上班，被铁路公安局、宾县公安局国保大队和胜利街派出所的警察抓捕，她家中的笔记本电脑、打印机、大法书籍、手机等被抄走。她被关押在哈尔滨第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，王健被依兰县检察院批捕。后遭起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、罚款十万元。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被哈尔滨市中级法院维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，王健被关押到黑龙江女子监狱八监区。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/2.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/2.html</span></b></a></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/5/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E5%B9%B4%E8%BD%BB%E5%A5%B3%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%B8%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E5%8B%92%E7%B4%A2%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%87%E7%BD%9A%E9%87%91-467885.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/5/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E5%B9%B4%E8%BD%BB%E5%A5%B3%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%B8%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E5%8B%92%E7%B4%A2%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%87%E7%BD%9A%E9%87%91-467885.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">40/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王立恒</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">:1979</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，山东省淄博市桓台县人，淄博市桓台县果里镇马王村<span lang="EN-US">187</span>号公民；香港占中运动支持者，“恶俗维基”及“支纳维基”二网站骨干成员，“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”受害人之一，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年起，中国大陆及海外有网友开始频繁尝试搭建和运作被称为“恶俗圈”的网络平台，其中“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”和“红岸基金会”三大网站最为知名；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年期间，其因与多人积极合作组建“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”二网站，随深受网站友人好评；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾因香港“占中”、要求“真普选”运动遭到中共当局授意下的港府严打，同时中国大陆《人民日报》又连续第<span lang="EN-US">18</span>天刊文批评占中运动，随于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日毅然赴香港金钟占领区，在天桥顶撑伞支持“占中”的学生及市民；但返回后不久，即被淄博市桓台县警方刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，又被山东省桓台县检察院以涉嫌“非法获取公民个人信息罪”予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被淄博市桓台县法院以“侵犯公民个人信息罪”和“非法获取国家秘密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因其又重回恶俗维基网站工作，而此时已有多家“恶俗圈”网站频发习近平之女习明泽、姐夫邓家贵的信息（含户籍和照片等个人信息），其所在“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”网站亦将此类信息挂于网上，遂立遭中共当局的打压迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，公安部迅速成立项目组，要求对全国该网站会员实施大抓捕；之后经严格审讯，发觉他们年龄尚小且行为基本无罪，故而各地警方将所抓之人纷纷予以释放，唯广东省茂名市警方想立功，声称要给中共建政<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年献大礼，遂移花接木嫁祸“恶俗维基”，把该警局所属的网站会员（含其在内）尽都抓捕，并上报公安部谎称“破获了一起与反华势力相勾结的恶势力集团大案”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被广东省茂名市警方跨省抓捕，并被指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”等转刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被茂名市检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪、侵犯公民个人信息罪”予以批捕；据悉曾因资料不足，而被检察院几次退侦和被地方法院数次退回要求重新起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人“涉恶势力犯罪集团案”被广东省茂名市茂南区法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其案<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人均被宣判，王立恒被该法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年），“侵犯公民个人信息罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月），二罪并罚，决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日；其等均表不服，已经上诉；二审维持原判。此前王立恒被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">41/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王玉杰：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，长春市绿园区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，家住长春市绿园区青年路春天花园二十号楼。<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年，王玉杰开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日上午八点左右，王玉杰和另一法轮功学员街上宣传法轮功，被警察绑架到派出所，随后被抄家，家里的真相币、所有的钱、大法书籍、播放器等被抢走。王玉杰在派出所被关押十二个多小时后放回。警察对她说，回家等着法院判决吧。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日又被警察抓捕，后获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，现已上诉到中级法院。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">42/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">王玉梅：辽宁</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年出生，辽宁省鞍山市人。她淳朴厚道，与老伴一起，来到居住在深圳市南山区的儿子家，帮忙带孙子。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，王玉梅在深圳市赠送法轮功资料，被南山区公安分局警察抓捕，南山区公安分局对她行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日下午，她在小区赠送邻里法轮功<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘，遭遇中共洗脑毒害的民众的恶告。当天晚上十点左右，王玉梅在家中被南山公安分局国保和南头派出所警察再次抓捕，关押到南山区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底，王玉梅被南山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。王玉梅认为此判决，提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，深圳市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/14/446204.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/14/446204.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">43/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许方泉：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东济南市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，济南钢铁集团（简称济钢，原为济南钢铁厂）管理技术人员，大学毕业，家住山东省济南市。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，许方泉去江苏连云港市女儿家探亲，他给路人赠送法轮功好的册子，被人举报，警察通过监控抓捕了许方泉。现被关押在连云港看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，江苏省连云港市海州区法院对许方泉开庭审理。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，许方泉被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://big5.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/25/%E5%B1%B1%E6%9D%B1%E7%9C%81%E6%BF%9F%E5%8D%97%E5%B8%82%E8%A8%B1%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%89%E5%9C%A8%E6%B1%9F%E8%98%87%E7%9C%81%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A9%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-464546.html"><b><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江大庆市林甸县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，大专文化，林甸县第二中学数学教师。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年开始炼法轮功。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2020</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，由黑龙江省公安厅“督办”，大庆市公安局和林甸县公安局出动五十多个便衣警察，暴力抓捕了大庆市林甸县法轮功学员薛丽威、王玉红、路朝波、董娜、陈卫波等。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，大庆让胡路区法院枉法判决：路朝波、王玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚款七万元。薛丽威、陈卫波被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚款四万元，董娜被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚款三万元。关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。薛丽威刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">45/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">燕宝萍</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：四川攀枝花市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生。原来是攀枝花机电学院校办会计，坚持信仰法轮大法，多次遭绑架、抄家，被开除工作；两次被非法劳教共四年，在四川资中楠木寺女子劳教所遭受到非人折磨。女儿被迫退学。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，燕宝萍在出租房内做法轮功资料时，被攀枝花市东区分局及临江路派出所警察抓捕。之后，燕宝萍被关押到盐边县看守所，后又被转入市看守所，现被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">46/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">尹兰华：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，吉林辽源市龙山区柏林小镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚间<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点多，辽源市向阳公安分局警察郭凯明等人侵入尹兰华的家中，搜查大法书、法轮功资料、法轮功币。尹兰华也被抓捕到向阳公安分局。那里的警察将她双手反背，用铁铐子铐上<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天，对她刑讯逼供后，最后将尹兰华关押到辽源市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月尹兰华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">47/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">余德贞：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宁夏石嘴山市惠农区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍在石嘴山市惠农区水城民生片区讲法轮功，贴真相不干胶，被国保大队和园艺派出所便衣警察跟踪抓捕、抄家，当晚三人被放回家。此后，警察便对每位法轮功学员进行暗中监控和跟踪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅等人被国保警察有预谋的抓捕、抄家。刘翠梅是从银川市的家中被警察抓捕到石嘴山市惠农区，在审讯过程中，多次被殴打。当天，余德贞、陈秀萍、史梅兰、刘翠梅被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅再被抓捕，在石嘴山看守所被关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，余德贞、陈秀萍、史美兰、刘翠梅被石嘴山市大武口区法院判刑。余德贞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被罚金三万元；陈秀萍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金二万五千元；史梅兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，被罚金一万元；刘翠梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">48/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曾加庚：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1942</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁，住广州市海珠区。他毕业于华南理工大学材料科学与工程学院高分子材料专业，原广州珠江轮胎有限公司高级工程师。退休前，他是单位的技术骨干。因为讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾加庚被公交分局侦查二大队警察跟踪抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，他被广州市检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底，他被劫入广东省四会监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/21/446562.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">49/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张立娟：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林伊通县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，吉林省伊通县法轮功学员张立娟和她儿子曹博宇分别在自家附近和家中被吉林省辽源市国保警察马队长等人秘密抓捕，关押在辽源市看守所。警察又抄家，劫走法轮功书籍、法相、资料、电脑、打印机、订书器等大量私人物品。曹博宇被关押近<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月左右被放回。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，辽源市西安区法院视频开庭，张立娟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">50/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚上十点多钟，张立云在日升村发放真相资料时，被村长刘景伟劫持到派出所。后被抓捕到拘留所、看守所，拒收；又被关押在公安局隔离。隔离之后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，又被关押到榆树市看守所。之后被构陷到德惠市检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张立云被德惠市法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，关押在到吉林省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">赵秀梅：</span></b></span><span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，没有通知家人的情况下，赵秀梅被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被送吉林省女子监狱八监区继续迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/8/452868.html#22127203045-1"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b lang="EN-US">30</span>日，邹建华在沈阳市皇姑区母亲的家中被警察抓捕，并抄走其电脑、打印机等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日其被辽中市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮大法后，杨顺梅因坚持法轮功信仰，坚持给民众宣传法轮功，于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年被劳教，于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">56/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">胡秀梅：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北沧州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚，河北沧州市法轮功学员胡秀梅、刘在云、苏春风、侯树元、、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人在新华区邓家屯村西口，被跟踪而至的新华区公安分局国保大队警察抓捕。后刘在云、胡秀梅、侯树元被关押沧州市看守所，苏春风因身体原因，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被“取保候审”回家。后四人均被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日侯树元、刘在云、苏春风和胡秀梅<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人遭运河区法院非法判刑：侯树元、刘在云遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金一万元；胡秀梅、苏春风遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金五千元。胡秀梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/26.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/26.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:
