_Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许冬青：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏市金坛区维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年遭黑社会暴力逼迁诱发心脏病，同时患有高血压等各种疾病，被医院诊断为有猝死风险，因和患疑难肾病的女儿杨丽一起到国家信访局上访反映资源部、公安部长年不处理江苏当地违法征地拆迁、公安对中国银行支行行长诈骗家属杨国良<span lang="EN-US">130</span>万元案压案不查等问题，遭到由原江苏省信访局局长（现省社会工作部部长）田洪和常州市市委书记陈金虎主使的打击报复。从<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月起，访民许冬青女士一直被金坛公安绑架拦截无法看病、上访。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，许冬青女士被逼向习近平求助，遭府右街派出所拦截，该所女警霍天一称向习近平求助不违法，但转身就让金坛区驻京办将许冬青女士截回。这次，他们以寻衅滋事为由刑事拘留了许冬青女士。许冬青被羁押在常州市看守所。</span></span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/72_6.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/72_6.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘杰：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1977</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，原在北京上班，军转干部，伤残警察。后迁户到西安至今未落户，现居住在山东省烟台市莱山区。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日晚上<span lang="EN-US">9:05</span>分刘杰在北京市丰台区西马场<span lang="EN-US">7</span>克拉<span lang="EN-US">6</span>号楼<span lang="EN-US">9</span>楼遭到很多不知什么地方的“民警”和不明身份的人反铐双手带走后，随即遭强迫失踪。后经其朋友们多地询问得知，刘杰已经于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被北京市公安局丰台分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，现在被羁押在北京市丰台区看守所。</span></span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/blog-post_6.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/blog-post_6.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">程晓峰：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">网名大卫，湖南株洲公民、民主人士、株洲公民圈活跃人士，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生于株洲，认同普世价值；曾就职于公安部门；在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年瘟疫爆发后，因公开站出来质疑当局核酸检测与疫苗问题，倍受社会关注，因此也受到了当局的恐吓与警告。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，在中共二十届三中全会召开之前，程晓峰被当地警方以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，羁押在湖南株洲市看守所。被带走前其居所和茶室均遭抄家搜查取证。据悉这次被捕的直接原因与他去娄底双峰祭拜欧阳经华、参与网络要求苏州纪念胡友平有关，也可能是湖南株洲当局对程晓峰多年民主异议言行算总账。</span></span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/blog-post_8.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/blog-post_8.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">尹旭安：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1974</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，湖北省大冶市人，原湖北省大冶市保安镇村民，公益维权公民，民主人士，政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，曾因控告湖北省鄂州市梁子湖区民政局就其夫妻离婚争议非法登记一案，被地方法院枉法裁判，而地方高院对此又不作为，随被迫于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年到北京上访；自<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月以来，因多次上访而备受当局非法处罚及伤害；曾因上访维权和参与围观、声援、抗争行动而被当局非法拘留<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次、被关黑监狱<span lang="EN-US">8</span>次；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，在美国时任总统奥巴马访华期间，曾因到北京市公安局治安总队申请游行示威，而被湖北当局处以劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并延期释放<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；劳教期间，曾因身患高血压三期（极高危程度）及多种其他疾病（如乙肝、胆囊炎及结石等）而多次晕倒和急救；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年起，曾因在京维权，开始更多关注民主公益维权事业；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，曾积极参与十八大民主直选学术代表，呼吁推进政治体制改革、废除劳教制度及打击黑监狱等；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾因举报和起诉湖北省当地政府非法征用土地、起诉湖北省劳教委非法延期及非法选举等问题，而遭当局非法拘禁<span lang="EN-US">42</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年始，开始积极介入声援围观行动，如江西新余刘萍独立候选人案、山东曲阜薛福顺事件、山东淄博孙峰“煽颠案”、<span lang="EN-US">4.29</span>祭奠林昭活动、湖南衡阳赵枫生“煽颠案”开庭、郑州十君子事件、焦作张小玉案、苏州老兵范木根血拆案开庭、与王福磊等维权网友声援维权公民王健案等。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因用微信转发“湖北大冶市驻京维稳人员名单”而遭当局抓捕，并被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被以涉嫌“泄露国家机密罪”刑拘，后被释放；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又因与王芳、耿彩文等维权人士在武汉市黄鹤楼前身着声援屠夫（吴凎）的文化衫，并拍照上传网媒，随于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被警方从家中带走，拘留于大冶市保安镇派出所，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被转为刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其案在湖北省大冶市法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；关押期间，曾遭狱警和牢头狱霸酷刑殴打，身心俱毁，且多次要求会见律师遭拒；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被减刑提前释放，但在出狱后不久的中共两会期间又被湖北省大冶市警方以涉嫌“故意泄露国家机密罪”刑拘，且遭虐待，直至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月才获释放；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，尹旭安因大冶市保安镇政法委书记袁启发，及金塘村党支记兼村长尹青松等人，在金塘村尹四房湾村民都没同意的情况下，不仅强行量了集体所有的、赖以生存的土地，并把挖掘机开到现场实施强征的不法行为而信访维权，然后就遭到一次次的打击报复，又被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其案被大冶市检察院起诉至地方法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其案被湖北省大冶市法院虽开庭审理，久拖至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日；据悉，其在狱中身体状况极差，已被抢救数次。尹旭安案二审<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日宣判维持原判四年半。此前在黄州监狱服刑。尹旭安在服刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月后于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日刑满获释后，一直遭软禁被限制人身自由，无法就医，后<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年初又遭强迫失踪，音信全无。家人至今无法联系他，也不知他在哪里，但据悉并未住院。尹旭安身患极高危高血压，曾因此在狱中数次病危，除非得到及时有效医疗，可能会随时再次中风，有生命危险。</span></span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/4_15.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/4_15.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><a name="_Hlk173156423"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8/</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173156423;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">昝爱宗</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">基督徒，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，安徽太和县人，杭州自由作家，国际笔会分会独立中文笔会（<span lang="EN-US">CIPC</span>）会员，倡导自由写作，自由出版。原中国海洋报记者、浙江记者站站长，被称为网上使用真名写作的自由作家，网名若干，如电子情、失语症患者、江南快客等，是新浪网专栏作家。著作及策划图书范围甚广。曾经在《南方周末》、《中国青年报》、《南风窗》等媒体发表文章。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，诺贝尔和平奖得主刘晓波逝世<span lang="EN-US">7</span>周年纪念日，独立中文笔会会员昝爱宗、庄道鹤和民主党人邹巍、毛庆祥、汪雪娥（吕耿松夫人）、程云惠（王东海夫人）、严忠良等共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人在浙江海宁钱塘江入海口举行海祭活动。活动的部分照片在网上发布。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因悼念刘晓波去世<span lang="EN-US">7</span>周年，浙江人权捍卫者昝爱宗被杭州市公安局拱墅区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，目前被羁押在杭州市拱墅区看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/7_21.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/7_21.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">邹巍：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">浙江民主党人。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，诺贝尔和平奖得主刘晓波逝世<span lang="EN-US">7</span>周年纪念日，独立中文笔会会员昝爱宗、庄道鹤和民主党人邹巍、毛庆祥、汪雪娥（吕耿松夫人）、程云惠（王东海夫人）、严忠良等共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人在浙江海宁钱塘江入海口举行海祭活动。活动的部分照片在网上发布。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因悼念刘晓波去世<span lang="EN-US">7</span>周年，浙江民主党人邹巍遭刑事拘留。</span></span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/7_47.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/7_47.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王默：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1972</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，江苏省淮安市人，网名“菜刀王默”，人称“黑犬”，民间知名新浪“转世党”，南方街头运动践行者，人权捍卫者，中国政治犯。近年来，因追求民主常在网上及南方街头发表积极言论而为民间所熟知，是近年走出网络开始参与现实抗争的典范；曾先后参与多起，诸如“曲阜薛福顺非正常死亡事件”、“新余刘萍等三人开庭声援围观”、“郑州十君子声援团”、“焦作张小玉事件调查”等大型抗争活动，遂遭到警方多次打压和被行政拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因在江西省新余刘萍等三人开庭时举牌声援，被警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，曾因在广东省广州市窖口地铁站旁举牌寻找民主维权人士张圣雨时，被警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾因在河南省焦作市参加张小玉事件调查活动，而被警方抓走并刑拘<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，再次因在广州市多地拉横幅声援香港民主抗争、“真普选”，被警方从广州市增城区新塘镇带走，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被广州市检察院更换罪名，以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式批捕，被关押在广州市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被广州市中级法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并送往韶关市乐昌监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出狱。获释一个月后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，又被江苏省淮安市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，被羁押于江苏省淮安市看守所。后音信全无。后维权朋友去探访王默父亲，方才获悉王默已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，关押到江苏省南京监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。获释后，王默仍然坚持发声，顽强不屈，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日王爱忠案在广州开庭，王默赴广州声援，随即被广州警方刑事拘留。关押三日后，被取保获释。王默<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日去杭州会友后第二天遭强迫失踪，后获悉王默于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日自杭州被淮安当地国保带回本地，软禁于淮安一酒店内，手机被扣，多人看管。但中共二十届三中全会已经闭幕多日，王默仍未见被释放，王默处于强迫失踪状态。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日获悉，王默已经被指定居所监视居住。</span></span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/19.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/19.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">11/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张盼成：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1995</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，甘肃省庆阳市合水县人，网名为“子慕予兮”，中国西北农村长大的留守儿童，前北京大学保安，政治犯。早年出生于甘肃农村，是典型的留守儿童；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾以公民身份表达自己的意愿；在辞去北京大学保安工作之后，曾放胆自拍视频，发政治主张，称已为民主“做好了牺牲的准备”；被捕前，曾在视频中表示，不同意中国政府将<span lang="EN-US">600</span>亿美元未经法定程序送<span lang="EN-US">(</span>外国）人，要求言论自由，声援被失踪的董瑶琼、华涌、佳士工人和原北大学生岳昕等人，以及进学习班的百万新疆同胞；曾在视频中引用宋代名将文天祥的诗句“人生自古谁无死，留取丹心照汗青”，并说自己对国家有深沉的爱；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，被抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被北京市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；审讯中，拒绝写保证书，并拒绝给律师签委托书；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其案在北京西城区法院开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被北京市西城区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因其在网上发布一段在甘肃山村老家里录制的视频，谴责中共暴行，表达心声称“凛凛寒冬终将过去，春天马上要来临”，遂被甘肃省合水县警方莫名刑拘，家遭查处，自此失联；后知又被当地合县检察院转正式批捕，被关押在甘肃省庆阳市合水县看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，知其已在两周前被甘肃省合水县法院一审秘判，但其家人未获判决书<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日获悉，其似被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。曾在甘肃省武都监狱（甘肃省武都区吉石坝武都监狱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">746000</span>）服刑。张盼成于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日刑满释放，张盼成回到家中后，屡遭当地警方骚扰和监控，出行自由遭剥夺，甚至想强迫做精神病检查。张盼成迫于无奈，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日就其状况发布了情况通报。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日的文中称，自己长期被跟踪，且身份证户口本均被没收，当地多次上门要将其认定为“精神病”，并表示如果自己再次被带走，将绝食抗议。近日，其遭强迫失踪，已失联多日，音信全无。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日获悉，张盼成已经被刑事拘留。</span></span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/35.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/35.html</span></b></a></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">五、</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New bold;">成孝宝、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：李芬、张爱泉、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年：</span></b></span><span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖北襄阳市法轮功学员，男，一九五七年七月二十八日出生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁，湖北襄樊人，原郑州铁路局襄樊铁路分局水电段水电工，家住湖北省襄阳市樊城区，一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。中共于一九九九年七月开始疯狂迫害法轮功。成孝宝因坚持修炼法轮功，多次被中共人员抓捕、关押。除此次被判十二年冤刑外，他还曾遭非法判刑、劳教共计五年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午，成孝宝等法轮功学员遭当地派出所警察抓捕，成孝宝被关押在行政拘留所。之后，外界再也没有成孝宝的信息。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月获悉，成孝宝多年前被当地中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，他被关押到湖北沙洋范家台监狱服刑，目前被非法关押在五监区。因为他长期拒绝戴监牌，拒绝当监狱苦力、完成各项奴工劳作，狱方就不准他休息，克扣他的饮食，长期罚站等各种体罚，不准他和别人说话。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/12.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: bold;">山西省忻州市保德基督教家庭教会成员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁。李艳萍于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被刑事拘留，罪名是组织他人偷越国边境罪，后被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，被关押在山西女子监狱，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月李艳萍的丈夫赵春旦透露说，目前他妻子李艳萍身体健康，就是有些缺钙。她在监狱里读不到圣经，加上记忆力变差，有时甚至记不起神的话。李艳萍在监狱里一直给周围的人传福音，目前已有七八位狱友愿意信主。李艳萍的父母<span lang="EN-US">80</span>多岁了，希望教会与家人替她照顾年迈的父母，为她尽孝。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。</span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; bold;">河北石家庄法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年大约<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，李晓岩，从石家庄乘火车回老家吉林省榆树市探亲，在石家庄火车站，李晓岩被查身份证，由于她在黑名单上，被火车站派出所拦下查包，发现真相币后被扣留。当天，石家庄市裕华区方兴派出所押解李晓岩回去抄家，抄走法轮功书籍、资料和真相币等物品。后李晓岩被关押在石家庄市第二看守所，被石家庄市铁路公检法构陷，遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。李晓岩不服判决，上诉到北京市第四中级法院（铁路法院）。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底被维持原判。目前其已被转监到石家庄女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁。一九九九年七月二十日，中共对法轮功残酷打压，她三次进京上访；两次被劳教，身心受到极大伤害。张君<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被国保警察从家中抓捕，关押，在不通知家人的情况下构陷、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，现在被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱集训队。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，家属去监狱看望张君。据悉，因她拒绝“转化”，三个月才能接见一次。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。</span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/4.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; lang="EN-US">26</span>日早，田丽丽在超市时，被新抚区公安分局警察抓捕，被劫持到新抚区千金派出所。田丽丽被强迫体检，因医生强行抽血而晕倒。之后，田丽丽被关押到抚顺市看守所。后获悉田丽丽被抚顺市东洲区法院判刑四<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，她被罚金一万六千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张继秋：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁，家住齐齐哈尔市铁锋区，一九九九年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月张继秋被铁锋区法院判刑九年，被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱，期间遭关小号、强行“转化”等酷刑迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，张继秋在家中被建华区卜奎派出所警察抓捕、关押到看守所，后来她被当地中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被转监黑龙江省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。</span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/4_18.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/4_18.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">盛丽</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：深圳市宝安区法轮功学员、企业家，女，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">48</span>岁。家住深圳市宝安区恒安花园。她来自辽宁省大连市，她大学毕业后，到深圳创业，很快办起了工厂，拥有了自己的外贸企业。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，她开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，盛丽跟人讲法轮功时，被监控拍到，遭宝安分局警察抓捕并抄家，后被关押到宝安看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，盛丽遭南山区法院判刑一年五个月，并罚金两千元。盛丽回家后，她顶着压力继续宣讲法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，盛丽向一个初中生赠送了一本法轮功期刊，随后被告发，其被抓捕刑拘，关押在深圳市宝安九围看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，盛丽被开庭，判刑四年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/4_28.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/4_28.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李芬：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">辽宁大连市法轮功学员，女，一九六七年七月十六日生，家住大连市甘井子区乾峰海景花园。一九九七年三月，李芬开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日李芬女士被抓捕，李芬被关押进大连市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，李芬被甘井子区法院庭审，庭审如同儿戏般，仅十分钟，草草结束，当庭没有宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，李芬的家属被告知，李芬被大连市甘井子区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金三万元。李芬不服一审判决，已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。</span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/36.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/36.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张爱泉：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省东营市法轮功学员，男。原是胜利油田滨海公安局交管中心的三级警督，一九九五年开始修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月中共发动了对法轮大法的迫害，张爱泉、王明云夫妇被当地警察列为重点人物，受到持续多年的残酷迫害，他们曾同时被非法判重刑，妻子王明云在狱中遭药物迫害，出狱后不久就含冤离世，张爱泉的父亲及岳父也因子女遭迫害受到沉重打击，先后离世。他因坚持法轮功信仰曾被判刑八年，被劳教三年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，山东省东营市公安局及胜利油田滨海公安局抓捕了多名法轮功学员，张爱泉在住所也被警察抓捕，一直被关押在滨海看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，东营市东营区法院对他判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。</span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/36_20.html"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">强小侠：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">陕西咸阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁。宝鸡市扶风县南阳镇南阳村人。一九九八年开始炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，强小侠将一封讲明法轮功真相的劝善信件交给双照派出所所长。同日下午被抓捕，拘留十天。至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，强小侠拘留期满又被刑事拘留，强小侠一直关押在咸阳市秦都看守所，期间身体左半身失去知觉，生活不能自理，后被彩虹公安分局送<span lang="EN-US">215</span>公安医院并要求家人陪护。其丈夫对公安人员说：“我妻子在家照顾年迈老人，身体好好的，现在被你们折磨成这样，还要我家里来照顾，你们还讲理吗？”后因公安强行要家里接人，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日强小侠被强行取保候审。强小侠于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被秦都区法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。她被威胁不得上诉，否则罚款。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/3.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/3.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郑荣珍：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖北省咸宁市温泉法轮功学员，女，退休会计，现年<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁。她长期遭受中共人员的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月份，郑荣珍女士在外发送法轮功资料时，被抓捕。后郑荣珍被关押到看守所。随后她的丈夫用钱以“取保候审”方式把她接回家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年秋，郑荣珍被咸安区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，随即被关押到武汉女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">13/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">湖北省咸宁市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，咸宁市煤化局职工。早年修炼法轮功，一九九九年七月二十日，中共江泽民集团开始公开迫害法轮功，因陈建平坚持修炼法轮功，遭到中共的残酷迫害，二十五年来，他六次被绑架、十次被关押、一次被判刑三年、三次被劳教共五年、四次被强制洗脑（两次被迫害得精神失常）、八次被抄家、一次被监视居住三个月、被勒索现金四千一百元、被抢劫现金四百元、工资损失十万元，累计直接经济损失十万四千五百元，还有电话被长期监听和骚扰，电脑等物品被抢劫一空，等等。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月上旬，陈建平发法轮功资料时，被摄像头拍到。陈建平随即遭抓捕抄家，陈建平被关押到拘留所，行政拘留十五天转刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月他被咸安区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。</span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/3_23.html</span></b></a></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">庞善喜：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省黑河市五大连池市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁，原是龙镇粮库职工，一九九九年开始修炼法轮功。庞善喜老人为了给五大连池市龙镇农场派出所警察宣讲法轮功，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份给这个派出所写一封劝善信。随即遭抓捕抄家，后被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，嫩江市法院对庞善喜判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款一万元。庞善喜老人先被关押到北安监狱，一个月左右被转关至黑龙江省泰莱监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/377.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/377.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">天津市滨海新区塘沽地区法轮功女学员，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被当地派出所警察抓捕、关押到天津市看守所。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，滨海新区法院先后两次庭审冉官权老人。现获知，她已被滨海新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、罚金八千元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。这是冉官权第二次遭司法迫害，十年前她曾被滨海新区法院法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/07/7526.html"><span mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">辽宁省葫芦岛市兴城法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生，一九九七年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，兴城市公安局闯进刘玉波家中，对其抄家和抓捕。在刘玉波体检不合格的情况下，公安警察强行将她关押到看守所。此次绑架起因是，五年前，刘玉波曾在兴城市碱厂乡宣传法轮功，被碱厂乡派出所非法抓捕，后被“取保候审”。此次刘玉波被抓捕，是公检法企图继续构陷她，进行所谓“结案”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，葫芦岛市法院判处刘玉波<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并罚金一万元。如今，被迫害七个半月的刘玉波，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被关押到辽宁省第二女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span></span><b><span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁，原宁夏宁光电工有限公司会计师，家住银川市兴庆区。一九九六年，她修炼法轮功。因不愿放弃修炼法轮大法，屡遭中共抄家、抓捕、关押等迫害，一到所谓的敏感时期，都是被骚扰的对象，电话长期被监听，出门就会被跟踪、盯梢，住所被监控。辛林原老太太<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被石嘴山市大武口区公安分局政保大队抓捕，关押在石嘴山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月上旬末，辛林原的丈夫陈建国收到了宁夏石嘴山市大武口区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。</span></span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><a lang="EN-US">2</span>月曾被判刑七年缓刑七年。王宋霞<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被宝鸡市公安局渭滨分局姜谭路派出所警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被“取保候审”放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初获悉：王宋霞已被当地法院判刑一年半、罚金五千元，六月她已被关押到陕西省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日下午，何明英从沈阳北站乘坐火车前往成都亲戚家。何明英刚上列车，数名警察就在未出示任何证件、也未告知缘由的情况下，对她强行搜身、检查包裹，然后将她劫持到沈阳北车站派出所。之后她被拘留十五天。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，沈阳市浑南区检察院以“证据不足”作出不批准逮捕决定。何明英本应被无条件释放，可是沈阳铁路公安国保警察却在何明英她作出“取保候审”的决定。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，何明英再次遭警察抓捕。沈阳市浑南区检察院于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日作出批捕决定，并于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被沈阳市浑南区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年、罚金两千元。何明英已于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日提起上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; _Hlk55009291;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">名在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">为了更方便人们查询本网统计的在押政治犯、良心犯的名单，本网每期随《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》一起发布《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》。本索引将本期报告所统计的人员名单，以人员姓名拼音字母排序（<span lang="EN-US">A</span>、<span lang="EN-US">B</span>、<span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk55009291;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">如您获知有未上名单的政治犯良心犯的境况，请随时向我们知会，<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">联系邮箱：<span lang="EN-US">wqw2011@gmail.com<o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span
